```
{
  "prompt": "Ultra-realistic selfie of a stunning young woman in her early 20s, western beauty with perfect symmetrical facial features, flawless glowing skin, sharp defined jawline, high cheekbones, large expressive almond-shaped blue eyes with dramatic long thick eyelashes and perfect winged eyeliner, perfectly shaped arched eyebrows, full glossy nude-pink lips, subtle rosy natural blush, long straight blonde hair styled in a sleek high ponytail, wearing large shiny gold hoop earrings, delicate diamond/bling rings and bracelet, white crisp button-up shirt slightly oversized with rolled sleeves, casually sipping a thick pink strawberry smoothie/frappuccino from a tall transparent Starbucks cup with pink straw, whipped cream and pink berry chunks visible on top, cup has classic green Starbucks logo, sunny day outdoor European/London-style street cafe terrace background with wooden tables, people sitting in the distance, classic brick and glass buildings, red awnings, warm golden hour sunlight, soft natural bokeh, selfie angle from slightly above eye level with arm extended, confident and chic vibe, luxurious casual fashion, photorealistic, 8k, highly detailed skin texture and pores, sharp focus, cinematic lighting, natural shadows",
  "negative_prompt": "blurry, low quality, deformed face, extra limbs, bad anatomy, cartoon, anime, illustration, plastic skin, overexposed, underexposed, text, watermark, ugly, distorted proportions, closed eyes, male, elderly, child, heavy makeup overload, neon colors, dark lighting, indoor, messy hair, no earrings, different drink, winter clothing",
  "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
  "style": "photorealistic",
  "lighting": "natural daylight, golden hour, soft shadows",
  "camera": "smartphone selfie, iPhone 15 Pro style, slight wide angle",
  "sampling_steps": 35,
```

### 3. Cozy-Sweet 棉花糖主题编辑肖像

**Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成异想天开、温馨甜美、带有俏皮柔和写实风格的编辑肖像的提示。它侧重于一个主体在游乐场与柔和的棉花糖互动，指定了高调照明、柔焦和鲜艳的“糖果”色彩，同时要求保留面部特征。

![Cozy-Sweet 棉花糖主题编辑肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544838272_6wvalg_G-qxp1NaYAAtPKG.jpg)
![Cozy-Sweet 棉花糖主题编辑肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544838407_gq0gz6_G-qxpz3bQAYr3NQ.jpg)

```
• Concept: Cozy-sweet editorial, face preserved, playful-soft realism.

• Story: Blowing bubbles or eating a giant pastel {argument name="cotton candy color" default="pastel"} cotton candy at a fair.

• Clothing: Oversized pastel knit sweater, pleated baggy.

• Accessories: Glitter on the cheekbones, colorful hair clips.

• Pose: Peering through the cotton candy, eyes wide and bright, slight playful pout.

• Lighting: Bright, soft "candy" colors, high-key lighting with no harsh shadows.

• Background: Blurred carnival lights, pastel-colored booths.

• Camera: 35mm, vibrant saturation, soft focus on the edges.

• Style: Whimsical, youthful, soft-focused skin and bright eyes.
```

### 4. Image-to-Image 姿态锁定和身份保留，适用于抹茶美学

**Author**: [Melis✨](https://x.com/miilesus)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: en

> 一个高度限制性的 JSON 提示，专为图像到图像生成而设计，要求参考姿势（侧身、交叉双腿、手部姿势）实现精确的 1:1 视觉匹配，同时将调色板调整为抹茶绿色美学。它使用严格的身份和姿势锁定约束，确保只改变面部身份和颜色，同时不允许出现特定的服装物品，如裤子或鞋子。

```
{
  "task_type": "image_generation_with_absolute_pose_lock",
  "edit_goal": "Generate an image that is an exact 1:1 visual match of the reference pose. Side-facing orientation, leg crossing, hand grip, and accessories must be identical. Only face identity and matcha color adaptation are allowed.",
  "global_locks": {
    "pose_lock": true,
    "side_orientation_lock": true,
    "leg_position_lock": true,
    "hand_grip_lock": true,
    "accessory_lock": true,
    "camera_lock": true,
    "allow_any_variation": false
  },
  "pose_definition": {
    "body_orientation": "Strict side-facing seated pose, not front-facing",
    "seating": "Sitting fully on a wooden bench, body turned sideways",
    "legs": {
      "crossing": "Legs crossed at the knee exactly as reference",
      "top_leg": "Angled forward and slightly upward",
      "bottom_leg": "Angled downward, resting naturally"
    },
    "leg_wear": {
      "type": "Sheer pantyhose",
      "color": "{argument name="tights color" default="matcha green"}",
      "opacity": "semi-sheer",
      "must_be_visible": true
    },
    "arms": {
      "primary_arm": {
        "position": "Bent at elbow",
        "height": "Chest level",
        "hand_action": "Holding a cup",
        "grip_style": "Side grip"
      },
      "secondary_arm": {
        "position": "Resting across the torso under the coat"
      }
    },
    "head": {
      "direction": "Facing sideways",
      "tilt": "Minimal"
    }
  },
  "appearance_constraints": {
    "visible_clothing_only": [
      "long fur coat",
      "matcha green tights"
    ],
    "fur_coat": {
      "style": "Luxury long faux fur",
      "color": "{argument name="coat color" default="matcha green"}"
    },
    "accessories": {
      "sunglasses": {
        "required": true,
        "style": "Dark fashion sunglasses",
        "position": "Worn on face"
      }
    },
    "disallowed_items": [
      "pants",
      "leggings",
      "dress",
      "skirt",
      "black tights",
      "brown tights",
      "shoes"
    ]
  },
  "object_constraints": {
    "drink": {
      "type": "Matcha",
      "cup": "Plain white takeaway cup",
      "position": "Held at chest level"
    }
  },
  "environment_constraints": {
    "location": "Elegant cafe exterior",
    "background": "Dark cafe facade with large glass doors",
    "bench": "Wooden bench",
    "lighting": "Natural daylight",
    "allow_change": false
  },
  "source_images": [
    {
      "id": "FACE_IMAGE",
      "role": "face_identity_reference"
    }
  ],
  "face_settings": {
    "identity_strength": 0.95,
    "expression_match": true,
    "skin_texture": "natural",
    "no_stylization": true
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "front facing",
    "looking at camera",
    "standing",
    "different leg position",
    "uncrossed legs",
    "missing sunglasses",
    "black tights",
    "brown tights",
    "pants visible",
    "shoes visible",
    "wrong hand grip",
    "cup held"
  ]
}
```

### 5. Image-to-Image Fusion for Identity and Attire Transfer

**Author**: [Mikasa](https://x.com/Mikasa_rose729)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: en

> 这是一个复杂的 JSON 格式提示，用于图像到图像融合工作流，优先考虑身份保留。它指示 AI 将“Ana de Armas”的面部身份从一张参考图像转移，并将完整的服装从第二张参考图像转移，将主体置于金色时段的高档户外露台环境中，并使用特定的相机和照明参数。

![Image-to-Image Fusion for Identity and Attire Transfer](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468550014_e3oobg_G-o6ONzbQAE2Wxx.jpg)

```
{
  "request_configuration": {
    "workflow": "image_to_image_fusion",
    "priority": "identity_preservation"
  },
  "source_references": {
    "primary_subject": {
      "id": "image_1",
      "target_element": "facial_identity",
      "subject_name": "{argument name="subject name" default="Ana de Armas"}",
      "constraints": "zero_morphing_policy"
    },
    "attire_reference": {
      "id": "image_2",
      "target_element": "full_outfit",
      "transfer_attributes": ["fabric_texture", "color_palette", "layering"]
    }
  },
  "generation_parameters": {
    "subject_specs": {
      "identity": {
        "face": "{argument name="face reference" default="Ana de Armas (reference image 1)"}",
        "features": "locked",
        "skin_texture": "hyper-realistic, detailed pores, natural blemishes"
      },
      "anatomy": {
        "pose": "dynamic three-quarter turn, hand resting on hip",
        "body_type": "consistent with Ana de Armas"
      },
      "styling": {
        "outfit": "cloned from image 2",
        "hair": "voluminous, natural wave, catching backlight"
      }
    },
    "environment_specs": {
      "setting": {
        "location": "upscale outdoor terrace",
        "background_depth": "deep_blur",
        "elements": ["soft architectural lines", "golden hour warmth", "vibrant greenery"]
      },
      "lighting": {
        "mode": "vibrant_high_key",
        "primary_source": "bright natural sunlight",
        "secondary_source": "soft rim lighting to separate subject from background",
        "hdr_profile": "ultra-high dynamic range"
      }
    },
    "camera_specs": {
      "optics": "85mm prime lens",
      "aperture": "f/1.8",
      "focus": "sharp on eyes",
      "quality_level": "4K UHD"
    }
  },
  "negative_prompt_constraints": [
    "facial distortion",
    "altered features",
    "low resolution",
    "dull lighting",
    "flat textures" Ratio 3.4 
  ]
}
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Celebrity Likeness]] [[85mm Lens Portrait]]

### 6. 逼真的编辑肖像，带参考锁定

**Author**: [Johnn](https://x.com/john_my07)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，用于生成一张逼真的编辑肖像（头像和肩膀），严格锁定与上传参考图像一致的面部特征、姿势和光照风格，同时允许将服装定制为中性色调的商务休闲装。

![逼真的编辑肖像，带参考锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468540919_426wld_G-ooloiaoAA2FIX.jpg)
![逼真的编辑肖像，带参考锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468540931_tago5e_G-oolpcbsAASbHE.jpg)
![逼真的编辑肖像，带参考锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468541873_8fycq7_G-oolr6agAALBQ3.jpg)

```
{
  "reference_usage": {
    "use_reference_for": [
      "face_identity",
      "facial_structure",
      "pose",
      "framing",
      "camera_angle",
      "lighting_style",
      "overall_composition"
    ],
    "do_not_copy": [
      "exact_outfit",
      "formal_corporate_styling",
      "celebrity_association"
    ]
  },
  "scene": {
    "type": "studio",
    "background": "soft_muted_gradient_with_subtle_texture",
    "lighting": "natural_soft_studio_lighting_with_gentle_falloff"
  },
  "subject": {
    "identity": "same_person_as_reference",
    "age_range": "late_20s_to_mid_30s",
    "pose": "relaxed_upright_head_and_shoulders_pose",
    "expression": "calm_confident_approachable_smile",
    "gaze": "direct_eye_contact_with_camera",
    "hair": {
      "style": "short_naturally_styled",
      "color": "dark_brown_or_black"
    },
    "facial_features": "match_reference_face_with_natural_variation"
  },
  "outfit": {
    "type": "smart_casual",
    "top": "solid_color_crewneck_or_lightweight_knit",
    "layer": "casual_blazer_or_unstructured_jacket",
    "colors": "{argument name="outfit colors" default="earthy_or_neutral_tones_beige_olive_charcoal"}",
    "styling": "effortless_and_modern_not_formal"
  },
  "camera": {
    "framing": "tight_head_and_upper_torso",
    "angle": "straight_on_or_slightly_above_eye_level",
    "lens": "85mm_portrait",
    "aperture": "f2.8",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow",
    "focus": "sharp_on_eyes_and_face"
  },
  "style": {
    "look": "photorealistic_editorial_casual_portrait",
    "skin_texture": "natural_detailed_realistic",
    "contrast": "soft_clean_with_warm_tones",
    "detail_level": "high"
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "formal_suit_and_tie",
    "corporate_headshot_style",
    "celebrity",
    "lookalike",
    "different_face_from_reference",
    "cartoon",
    "illustration",
    "overprocessed_skin",
    "blur",
    "low_resolution"
  ]
}
```

### 7. 商业时尚摄影与严格的服装保护（变体）

**Author**: [Amanpreet Singh](https://x.com/amanxdesign)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，与另一个条目高度相似，用于生成一张高端商业生活方式照片。它严格要求保留参考图像中服装的精确细节，照片中一位白人美国女性模特以自然、自信的姿势置身于户外城市人行道场景中，沐浴在柔和的自然日光下。

![商业时尚摄影与严格的服装保护（变体）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468559362_k4ws2l_G-KBiSEa0AIEyjV.jpg)
![商业时尚摄影与严格的服装保护（变体）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468559720_lrqbj9_G-KBiSRa0AAnCq2.jpg)

```
{
  "task_configuration": {
    "type": "GENERATE",
    "sub_type": "commercial_lifestyle_photograph",
    "reference_logic": "STRICT_GARMENT_PRESERVATION_FROM_INPUT",
    "aesthetic": "high_end_fashion_campaign",
    "output_quality": "high_resolution_photorealistic"
  },
  "subject_definition": {
    "identity": {
      "demographic": "white American female model",
      "physique": "fit",
      "appearance": "beautiful, naturally styled"
    },
    "skin_and_features": {
      "realism_rule": "macro_level_human_realism; NO artificial smoothing or filtering",
      "texture_details": [
        "visible natural pores",
        "light blemishes and imperfections",
        "soft expression lines around eyes/mouth",
        "light freckles across nose/cheeks",
        "natural skin highlights and subsurface scattering"
      ],
      "makeup": "minimal, natural or bare skin look"
    },
    "attire_constraints": {
      "source": "garment_from_input_reference_image",
      "preservation_rules": [
        "exact color dye and pattern",
        "exact fabric weave and texture",
        "exact thread stitching details",
        "exact fit, drape, and silhouette on the body"
      ],
      "modification_permission": "NONE"
    },
    "pose": {
      "framing": "full_body_standing",
      "style": "natural, relaxed, confident",
      "orientation": "facing camera to showcase garment front"
    }
  },
  "environment_definition": {
    "location_type": "outdoor_urban_sidewalk",
    "specific_context": "outside a stylish cafe or artisan building facade",
    "contextual_logic": "architecture and decor must visually complement the style of the reference clothing",
    "atmosphere": "elevated, authentic city life, cinematic quality",
    "background_elements": [
      "textured building materials (brick, stone, wood)",
      "cafe seating or planter boxes",
      "pavement textures"
    ]
  },
  "composition_and_layout": {
    "camera_principles": [
      "commercial fashion standards",
      "golden ratio alignment of subject",
      "product-centered focus",
      "grid alignment"
    ],
    "framing_scale": "wide full shot (head to toe)",
    "spatial_margins": {
      "top_margin": "generous clear space above head for potential typography/cropping",
      "side_margins": "balanced clear space",
      "bottom_margin": "clear space below feet"
    }
  },
  "lighting_and_optics": {
    "source": "natural daylight",
    "quality": "soft, diffused sunlight or open shade",
    "color_temperature": "warm undertones",
    "shadows": "clean, natural falloff defining form without harshness"
  },
  "constraints_and_prohibitions": {
    "must_not_render": [
      "airbrushed skin",
      "plastic textures",
      "studio backdrop",
      "altered clothing design",
      "overly posed look"
    ]
  }
}
```

### 8. 电影浪漫编辑：阳台花卉交换

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-01-14  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，用于生成一张电影般的浪漫编辑图片：两个人站在地中海风格的相对阳台上，跨越间隙交换一束鲜花。该提示强调强烈的建筑对称性、广阔的负空间（蓝色天空），并严格遵循参考图像的构图和身份。

![电影浪漫编辑：阳台花卉交换](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468548999_npwu7j_G-np911bIAABq-f.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "photoreal_cinematic_romantic_editorial",
      "version": "v1.0_BALCONY_TO_BALCONY_FLOWERS_REACH_BLUE_SKY",
      "priority": "highest"
    },

    "references": {
      "reference_image_1": {
        "source": "UPLOAD_REFERENCE_IMAGE",
        "purpose": "COMPOSITION_AND_STORY_REFERENCE",
        "strict_lock": true,
        "match_reference_priority": "MAX",
        "preserve_symmetry_and_negative_space": true,
        "preserve_balcony_architecture": true,
        "preserve_subject_positions": true,
        "preserve_action_gesture": true,
        "no_style_drift": true
      },
      "reference_image_2": {
        "source": "UPLOAD_FACE_REFERENCE (OPTIONAL)",
        "purpose": "FACE_IDENTITY_LOCK_FEMALE",
        "strict_lock": true,
        "face_similarity_priority": "MAX",
        "no_identity_blending": true,
        "no_beautify": true,
        "no_age_shift": true,
        "preserve_skin_texture": true,
        "preserve_facial_proportions": true
      },
      "reference_image_3": {
        "source": "UPLOAD_FACE_REFERENCE (OPTIONAL)",
        "purpose": "FACE_IDENTITY_LOCK_MALE",
        "strict_lock": true,
        "face_similarity_priority": "MAX",
        "no_identity_blending": true,
        "no_beautify": true,
        "no_age_shift": true,
        "preserve_skin_texture": true,
        "preserve_facial_proportions": true
      }
    },

    "creative_direction": {
      "concept": "A cinematic romantic editorial shot: two people on opposite balconies reach across an open sky gap, one offering a bouquet of soft pink flowers. Minimalist, poetic, and visually striking with strong symmetry and expansive negative space.",
      "mood": "tender, playful, sunlit, modern romance",
```

### 39. 油画风格参考人物自画像

**Author**: [ひいらぎまる](https://x.com/hiiragimaruru)  **Date**: 2026-01-12  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂多段提示，它指示 AI 使用参考图像锁定角色的身份（面部、服装、颜色），然后生成一个场景，其中该角色在艺术工作室中以经典、有纹理的油画风格绘制自己的自画像。

![油画风格参考人物自画像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319236800_asbs6a_G-ejDygaMAAB8kw.jpg)

```
【入力画像】
画像1：参照キャラクター（このキャラクターの外見を絶対に変えないこと）

【最優先ルール：Identity Lock（外見固定）】
- 参照画像のキャラクターの「顔」「髪型」「髪色」「目の形/色」「肌色」「体型比率」「服装」「アクセサリー」「模様」「色配置」を100%一致させる。
- 表情も画像1と同じに保つ（※どうしても変える必要がある場合でも“ごく僅か”に）。
- 新しい小物・服・装飾を勝手に追加しない。髪を伸ばす/短くする等の改変禁止。年齢・性別・体格・種族感を変えない。
- 変更してよいのは「ポーズ」「背景（場所）」「ライティング」「画角」「画材（筆/パレット/イーゼル等の小道具）」のみ。

【生成したいシーン】
画像1のキャラクターが、絵画アトリエでイーゼルの前に立ち、油絵で“自分自身の肖像画”を描いている。
- 右手に筆、もう片方の手にパレット。
- 机に油絵具のチューブ、溶き油、筆洗い瓶、布、汚れたパレット、床に少し散った絵具跡。
- キャンバスには「描きかけの自画像」があり、画像1と“同じキャラクター”だと一目で分かる（同じ顔・同じ髪・同じ服・同じ配色）。描きかけなので少しラフな筆致でOK。

【画風（全体の表現）】
- 作品全体をクラシックな油絵として描写。キャンバス地の目、厚塗り（インパスト）筆致、絵具の盛り上がり、グレージングの深み。
- ただしキャラクターデザイン（線/形/色/特徴）は画像1から絶対に崩さない。油彩の質感は“上塗り”として付与するイメージ。

【構図・カメラ】
- 3/4アングルのミディアムワイド（上半身〜膝くらいまで）。キャラクター＋イーゼル＋キャンバスが同時に見える。
- 暖かい午後の斜光が窓から入り、顔とキャンバスに当たる。背景はやや暗めで主役が浮き立つ。

【出力指定】
- 1枚の画像。縦長 2:3
- 画像内に文字は入れない。
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Fine Art Portrait]]

### 47. 高定时装影棚肖像，严格锁定身份

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-01-12  **Language**: en

> 这是一个极其详细、技术性强的提示，用于生成一张奢华高级时装工作室肖像。它要求严格锁定基于上传参考图像的面部身份，确保面部结构或皮肤纹理没有任何变化。场景指定了精确的相机设置（85mm 定焦镜头，f/4 光圈）、干净的工作室照明（大型柔光箱主光）和造型（黑色深 V 领连衣裙，大胆的金色链条项链），背景为纯白色。

Floating water particles are visible between the camera and Subject, with slight refraction distortion around mask edges and hands.

```
The image should feel like a real close-distance snorkeling travel photo intimate, immersive, and authentic.
```

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细 JSON 提示，旨在生成一张女性在厨房里的超逼真生活方式图像，她微笑着看向镜头，怀里抱着一个滑稽的超大金属烹饪勺，强调自然光线并保留参考图像中的人物特征。

![厨房里女人抱着巨型勺子的写实照片提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319225951_in9vzj_G-buqUMa8AAwVr_.jpg)

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "language": "en",
  "style": "photorealistic lifestyle photography",
  "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_reference_image": true,
    "strict_identity_lock": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "alter_features": false,
    "notes": "Preserve the subject’s facial features, proportions, skin texture, hair, age, and gender exactly as in the reference image."
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "the subject’s own kitchen",
    "background": [
      "visible kitchen cabinets",
      "countertops",
      "everyday kitchen details"
    ],
    "lighting": {
      "type": "natural daylight",
      "source": "window light",
      "effect": "soft, realistic illumination across the scene"
    }
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "pose": {
      "position": "standing",
      "body_language": "relaxed and natural",
      "hands": "both hands wrapped around a giant metal spoon held in front of the body"
    },
    "expression": "smiling naturally while looking directly at the camera",
    "wardrobe": {
      "top": "brown knitted sweater",
      "bottom": "blue denim jeans"
    },
    "prop": {
      "object": "giant metal cooking spoon",
      "scale": "almost as tall as the subject",
      "material": "shiny polished metal",
      "interaction": "the subject hugs the spoon with both arms"
    }
  },
  "camera": {
    "shot_type": "full or medium-full body shot",
    "angle": "eye-level",
    "focus": "sharp focus on the subject and spoon",
    "depth_of_field": "natural depth with background slightly softened"
  },
  "quality": {
    "realism": "highly realistic, natural photo look",
    "details": "clear textures of clothing, metal spoon, and kitchen elements"
  },
  "constraints": [
    "No artificial lighting effects",
    "No stylization or fantasy elements",
    "No distortion of proportions",
    "No text, logos, or watermarks"
  ],
  "output_goal": "Create a natural, photorealistic photo of a woman standing in her own kitchen, smiling at the camera while holding an oversized shiny metal spoon, illuminated by soft daylight coming through a window."
```

### 58. 复古影棚肖像与身份保留提示词

**Author**: [Harboriis](https://x.com/harboriis)  **Date**: 2026-01-12  **Language**: en

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供的详细提示，旨在生成一张垂直中景工作室肖像，具有受 70/90 年代胶片摄影（柯达 Portra）启发的温暖怀旧美学。它强调保留参考照片中人物的精确面部特征和表情，同时让主体身着柔和的军绿色调服装，置身于深绿色织物背景前。

![复古影棚肖像与身份保留提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319138541_0vvq4d_G-bl9pDaEAAawfx.jpg)

```
MAIN SUBJECT (IDENTITY)

Use the person from the reference photo as the main subject. Keep their exact facial features, hairstyle, skin tone, and expression perfectly unchanged preserve all realism, emotional depth, and subtle facial lighting. Allow changes only in camera position, background motion, and atmosphere.

SCENE & COMPOSITION

Vertical medium-shot studio portrait. The man sits on a simple wooden or metal stool, gentle half-profile torso turn. One leg crossed over the other for a relaxed, composed posture; hands resting naturally. Overall mood: quiet, calm, restrained.

CLOTHING

Shirt (top layer): Oversized shirt in faded olive, dusty khaki, or washed military green. Soft textured cotton, sleeves rolled to mid-forearm, natural subtle wrinkles. T-shirt (underlayer): Washed charcoal matte tee, no logos, slightly fitted under the shirt. Trousers: Wide-leg trousers in deep charcoal or washed black; matte heavy-duty cotton or wool blend, straight lines, minimal folds. Accessories: None or very minimal-eg. simple old-style metal watch.

BACKGROUND

Heavy matte fabric backdrop (velvet or thick cotton) in deep forest green, warm olive, or muted army green. Soft draping with subtle folds; warm gradient fall-off toward the edges.

LIGHTING

Warm nostalgic studio lighting (4500-5000K). Large softbox for wraparound illumination. Soft golden skin highlights, lifted shadows for a matte non-contrasty look. Mild rim light along cheek and hair; faint vignette around edges. Mood inspired by 70s early 90s studio portraits.

CAMERA/OPTICAL LOOK

85mm vintage portrait lens, f/2.8 depth of field. Soft micro-contrast, slight halation, very fine film grain, matte warm-muted profile.

COLOR/STYLE

Warm nostalgic palette with muted military tones: golden skin, faded olive, dusty khaki, charcoal. Matte texture, lifted blacks, compressed highlights, subtle organic film grain. Overall: soft warm film portrait with restrained post-war aesthetic, Kodak Portra-inspired
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Studio Portrait]] [[Kodak Portra Film]]

### 59. 奢华情侣专题活动的分层 JSON 提示

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-01-11  **Language**: en

> 一个高度受限的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的奢华时尚专题照片，描绘一对情侣在艺术博物馆内。它要求严格匹配参考图像中的身份和姿势，指定了高级时装（无肩带白色迷你连衣裙、定制黑色西装），并详细描述了场景（坐在古典画作下的画廊长凳上，阅读抽象报纸），采用柔和的博物馆灯光，营造出精致的宣传效果。

![奢华情侣专题活动的分层 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768225963745_z6cly1_G-arYnXXAAA3Gbg.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "photorealistic_couple_editorial_campaign",
      "version": "v1.2_MUSEUM_LUXURY_COUPLE_EDITORIAL",
      "priority": "highest"
    },
    "references": {
      "reference_image_1": "UPLOAD_REFERENCE_IMAGE (POSE + COMPOSITION + MOOD LOCK)"
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "2:3",
      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "ultra_photoreal_high_fashion_editorial",
      "sharpness": "crisp_but_natural",
      "film_grain": "none_or_minimal",
      "color_grade": "warm_museum_luxury_true_to_life"
    },
    "hard_constraints": [
      "EXACTLY 2 people only (one woman, one man).",
      "Perfect identity match if faces are provided (no face or body changes).",
      "Pose and framing must match the reference: seated side-by-side on a gallery bench, relaxed crossed-leg posture.",
      "No readable text, no logos, no watermarks (newspapers must be blank or abstract).",
      "Perfect anatomy: hands, fingers, legs, feet, and posture fully correct.",
      "Photoreal skin texture; no plastic smoothing.",
      "No extra people, reflections, or background faces."
    ],
    "creative_prompt": {
      "scene_summary": "Ultra-photoreal luxury fashion editorial set inside a high-end art museum or gallery. A stylish couple sits casually on a wooden gallery bench beneath a large framed classical landscape painting. The woman wears a strapless white mini dress with a sculpted silhouette, white high heels, and elegant sunglasses; hair pulled back in a refined updo; minimal gold jewelry. The man wears a tailored black suit with a white shirt and dark sunglasses; polished shoes; relaxed but confident posture.\n\nBoth are reading newspapers in a playful, ironic editorial moment; all newspaper pages are visually abstract with NO readable text or headlines. Composition mirrors the reference: balanced symmetry, legs crossed, effortless elegance. Lighting is soft museum gallery lighting—warm, diffused, shadow-controlled—creating a refined cinematic atmosphere. Color palette: warm neutrals, ivory walls, golden frame accents, natural wood tones. Mood: chic, intellectual, modern luxury, quietly confident, fashion-house campaign quality.\n\nCamera: 85mm editorial portrait look, medium depth of field, subjects tack sharp, background painting slightly softened but recognizable. Overall feel: Vogue / luxury brand campaign, timeless and sophisticated."
    },
    "negative_prompt": [
      "any readable text",
      "logos, branding, watermarks",
      "extra people or reflections",
      "distorted legs, hands, feet",
      "identity drift",
      "cartoon, anime, CGI look",
      "plastic or over-smoothed skin",
      "harsh flash or blown highlights",
      "busy or cluttered background",
      "cheap fashion styling"
    ]
  }
}
```

### 64. 电影感闪光摄影夜间专题

**Author**: [Mayuri~](https://x.com/twocellz)  **Date**: 2026-01-11  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超现实、高对比度的肖像，采用闪光摄影美学，模拟狗仔队或夜间社论风格。画面中一位女性身着黑色缎面紧身胸衣和超短裙，坐在一间黑暗的豪华休息室里，并严格锁定参考图像以保持身份一致。

![电影感闪光摄影夜间专题](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768226060746_vx3wi1_G-ZkwDCa0AAt6hJ.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_type": "Cinematic Flash Photography Portrait (Reference Character)",
  "style": [
    "hyper-realistic",
    "flash photography aesthetic",
    "vogue night editorial",
    "high contrast",
    "sharp details"
  ],
  "subject": {
    "identity": "Use the same woman from the provided reference image",
    "consistency": [
      "maintain identical facial structure",
      "preserve skin tone and complexion",
      "match eye shape, nose, lips, and facial proportions",
```

### 101. 街头风格人像，带身份锁定和特定姿势

**Author**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc)  **Date**: 2026-01-08  **Language**: en

![高对比度特写，严格聚焦身份和纹理](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967445546_m4enjm_G-J0uqRXEAA1B5e.jpg)

```
(3:4). A raw, high-contrast close-up [Snapshot] captured with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. The entire frame is SHARP and in focus, from the fuzzy textile fibers to the skin texture.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics: visible micro-pores, a natural "satin-finish" healthy hydration glow, and fine vellus hair catching the light.
Silhouette Calibration (CRITICAL): Prioritize the dominant structural bust volume and the aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist. Focus on the high-impact anatomical depth and symmetry of the upper torso.
Outfit & Textural Interaction:

Clothing: She wears an oversized, heavy-weight Black Fuzzy Mohair Cardigan with a deep, open front.
Inner Detail: Beneath the cardigan, she wears a minimalist black garment featuring two ultra-thin 2mm black "V" shaped elastic straps that frame her décolletage.
Physicality & Tension: Her RIGHT HAND (featuring white manicured nails) is reaching forward, grabbing and pulling the fuzzy fabric of the cardigan together, creating realistic tension lines and textural bunching. The thin black straps show extreme elastic tension, creating a subtle, natural indentation against her fit form.
Pose & Composition:

Pose: A tight, front-on close-up shot focused on the upper torso and décolletage. Her long, dark chestnut hair is draped over her shoulders, framing the scene.
Geometry: The high-angle perspective highlights the structural volume and the 3D depth created by the contrast between the dark fuzzy fabric and her radiant skin.
Environment & Lighting:

Lighting: Brutal, Direct Afternoon Sunlight. The sun creates high-contrast highlights on the mohair fibers and her skin, casting sharp, defined shadows under the bust and within the folds of the cardigan.
Background (SHARP): A minimalist, neutral grey-toned matte wall. Every texture and grain of the wall is perfectly IN FOCUS. No artificial depth-of-field.
Quality: Raw unedited social-media "fit-check" aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible digital grain in the deep shadows, 8k resolution.
```

### 128. Kindergarten Crayon Doodle Illustration Prompt

**Author**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u)  **Date**: 2026-01-02  **Language**: en

> A highly detailed image generation prompt designed to convert an uploaded identity reference (person) into an ultra-cute, kindergarten-style crayon doodle illustration. The prompt specifies style, color, texture, facial features, proportions, and rendering rules to ensure a warm, childlike, and innocent aesthetic while strictly preserving the subject's identity.

![Kindergarten Crayon Doodle Illustration Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508430191_gfllqe_G9r1zAhbEAA_Ohs.jpg)
![Kindergarten Crayon Doodle Illustration Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508430983_mbvjqc_G9r1zAiasAAsoS5.jpg)

```
Use the uploaded image strictly as the identity reference. Preserve the same person, facial structure, hairstyle, age, gender, body proportions, and likeness exactly. Do not add or remove any person. Do not change identity. Convert the subject into an ultra-cute kindergarten-style crayon doodle illustration.

Illustration Style:
Hand-drawn kindergarten doodle made with crayons and soft colored pencils. Lines should be thick, rounded, uneven, and slightly shaky, like a small child’s drawing. Outlines are imperfect, playful, and soft, never sharp or clean.

Color & Texture:
Bright pastel crayon colors with soft, chalky texture. Flat coloring with visible crayon grain and overlapping strokes. Colors may go slightly outside the lines to enhance the childlike feel. No realistic gradients; only simple color fills and soft watercolor-like blobs.

Facial Features:
Very simple and adorable facial features. Big round dot eyes, tiny curved smile, minimal or no nose. Cheeks can have soft pink crayon circles. Expression should feel innocent, happy, and friendly.

Proportions & Form:
Chibi-like doodle proportions — large head, small rounded body, short arms and legs. Hands and feet are simple mitten or oval shapes. Anatomy should look intentionally naive and cute.

Shading & Lighting:
No realistic lighting. No depth or shadows. If needed, add light pastel crayon scribbles under the character for grounding only.

Mood & Atmosphere:
Sweet, cozy, wholesome, and joyful. Feels like an illustration from a nursery book or a child’s school drawing. Very warm and comforting emotional tone.

Background:
Simple doodle background with crayon-drawn clouds, sun, stars, hearts, flowers, or soft scribbles. Use light pastel paper tones. Background must remain minimal and playful.

Rendering Rules:
No photorealism, no photo texture, no cinematic lighting, no digital painting, no anime, no manga, no 3D, no vector art. Everything must look hand-drawn with crayons and pencils.

Final Output:
An ultra-cute kindergarten-style crayon doodle illustration with childlike proportions, playful pastel colors, and innocent expressions, maintaining the exact identity from the uploaded image in a warm children’s storybook style.
```

[[Identity Preservation]]

---

### 129. Scribbly Doodle Illustration Style Prompt

**Author**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u)  **Date**: 2026-01-02  **Language**: en

> A detailed image generation prompt designed to transform an uploaded identity reference into a messy, fun, scribbly doodle-style illustration. The prompt specifies rough, energetic line art, flat pastel colors, exaggerated features, and a chaotic, carefree mood, while strictly preserving the subject's identity and likeness.

![Scribbly Doodle Illustration Style Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508416318_5u85f1_G9rzkk6aoAA3ooW.jpg)

```
Use the uploaded image strictly as the identity reference. Preserve the same person, exact facial structure, hairstyle, age, gender, body proportions, and overall likeness. Do not add or remove any person. Do not change identity. Transform the subject into a messy, fun, scribbly doodle-style illustration.

Doodle Illustration Style:
Create a hand-drawn doodle with uneven, rough, and exaggerated line art. The lines should be loose, wobbly, and erratic, like a child’s excited scribble. Outlines should be thick, broken, and inconsistent. The drawing style must look rushed, spontaneous, and energetic. Use visible pencil or crayon strokes that add to the untidy, chaotic feel.

Color & Texture:
Use bright, pastel, and vivid colors in a flat, playful way. The color should be filled in without careful detail, mimicking a rough, sketchbook feel. The colors must look uneven and imperfect, almost like they’ve been scribbled on quickly. Add some watercolor textures, but keep them playful and imperfect, as if someone has used a wet brush for a quick, vibrant fill.

Facial Features:
Draw simple, exaggerated, childish features. Dot eyes, tiny squiggly smiles, and tiny noses. Keep the features rough and uneven, adding to the playful, messy doodle effect. Expressions should be lively and fun, filled with joy.

Proportions & Form:
Slightly exaggerated proportions with a large head, simplified limbs, and soft, rounded body shapes. The anatomy should look very stylized and unrealistic. Add extra randomness to proportions, with some body parts bigger or smaller than usual.

Shading & Lighting:
No realistic shading. Use rough pencil strokes for shading or simple color blobs. The lighting should be minimal, keeping the whole image bright and flat without depth.

Mood & Atmosphere:
Fun, quirky, and full of energy. The vibe should be carefree and spontaneous, like a doodle drawn in the middle of a storybook or a school notebook. Keep the emotional tone playful and full of life.

Background:
The background should be a mix of simple, scribbly shapes, soft doodle marks, and abstract forms like squiggles, hearts, stars, or random lines. Keep the background as loose and unrefined as the subject.

Rendering Rules:
No photorealism, no photo texture, no cinematic lighting, no digital painting. The illustration should look like a true, chaotic, scribbly doodle. Avoid sharp or clean edges, avoid detailed realism. The lines and colors must be rough and spontaneous.

Final Output:
A lively, fun, and messy scribbly doodle-style illustration using crayon or colored pencil, with rough, energetic lines and flat pastel colors, preserving the exact identity from the uploaded image in a playful, carefree doodle style.
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Image-To-Image Generation]]

### 144. 一次性相机派对肖像提示

**Author**: [simply](https://x.com/kingofdairyque)  **Date**: 2025-12-31  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张坦率、怀旧的肖像，风格为摄影师 Petra Collins，模拟一次性相机闪光灯的强烈美学效果，其中包含“2026”水钻太阳镜和金属派对气球等特定配饰，同时将发型锁定到参考照片。

![一次性相机派对肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767456138712_1s1ore_G9exRczaYAApj-R.jpg)
![一次性相机派对肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767456140133_ibr4qk_G9exRf0b0AAo-LV.jpg)

```
Use this photo attached to create a disposable camera–inspired candid portrait in the style of Petra Collins.
Hair (LOCKED – must remain identical every time):
As the reference photo 
Expression & Face:
Playful, slightly pouty candid expression. Eyes glance upward with a mildly bored, unserious, spontaneous look—not posed. Lips softly pursed. Natural skin texture visible, minimal makeup with soft blush and natural lip tone, no heavy retouching.
Pose & Framing:
Casual upper-body snapshot framing. Subject slightly off-center, shoulders relaxed, body angled subtly. Arms rest naturally close to the torso. Feels like a quick party photo taken mid-moment.
Attire & Accessories (high detail):
Wearing a simple fitted black spaghetti-strap top, casual and understated. Fabric reflects the flash subtly with slight sheen. No statement jewelry—focus remains on hair, expression, and accessories.
Sunglasses (DETAILED – 2026):
Oversized black plastic party sunglasses resting on top of the head. The lenses feature bold rhinestone-style numbers spelling “{argument name="year" default="2026"}”, evenly spaced across both lenses. The numbers sparkle harshly under direct flash, with uneven reflections, tiny blown highlights, and visible plastic texture. Sunglasses sit slightly crooked, reinforcing the candid, unpolished party feel.
Lighting & Camera:
Shot using a cheap 35mm disposable film camera. Direct on-camera flash only—harsh, flat, frontal lighting. Overexposed highlights on skin, hair, sunglasses, and balloons. Deep shadows behind the subject. Visible grain, slight blur, imperfect focus, no digital sharpness.
Background & Balloons (highly detailed):
Metallic foil fringe curtain in the background with silver and pastel reflections. Large metallic number balloons float nearby, partially cropped by the frame. Balloons show realistic seams, wrinkles, and creases, reflecting the flash with distorted highlights. Thin curling balloon strings hang unevenly, adding clutter and realism.
Color & Texture:
Slight film color cast, saturated but imperfect tones. Whites slightly blown, blacks mildly crushed. Strong grain throughout, soft edges, subtle color inconsistencies typical of disposable film.
Overall Mood:
Intimate, nostalgic, playful, and unfiltered—feels like a real late-night party snapshot taken by a friend, not a styled shoot.
Style Keywords:
Petra Collins inspired, disposable camera flash, candid party portrait, 2026 sunglasses, metallic balloons, foil fringe backdrop, 35mm film grain, imperfect framing, nostalgic realism
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Flash Photography]] [[Nostalgic Aesthetic]]

### 152. 在 Fairmont Hairpin 拍摄的年轻女性高端生活方式编辑图片提示

**Author**: [Abbay](https://x.com/LearnWithAbbay)  **Date**: 2025-12-30  **Language**: en

> 这是一个高度详细、结构化的图像生成提示，可能用于高端生活方式社论或时尚摄影。它详细说明了拍摄对象的样貌、服装、姿势、动作、地点（费尔蒙发夹弯）、灯光、构图，甚至包括赛道护栏的特定排版细节，以确保非常精确的视觉输出。

![在 Fairmont Hairpin 拍摄的年轻女性高端生活方式编辑图片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455008566_onopgw_G8lx5_XbwAEgjDP.jpg)

```
{
  "subject": {
    "person": "{argument name="person description" default="Young woman, early 20s, Caucasian"}",
    "hair": "Warm blonde hair, softly waved with airy movement",
    "pose": "Standing near railing, head turned slightly toward track",
    "expression": "Relaxed, confident, subtle smile"
  },
  "outfit": {
    "top": "Ivory off-shoulder fitted top",
    "bottoms": "High-waisted cream trousers",
    "accessories": "Mini bag, delicate necklace, minimalist earrings"
  },
  "action": {
    "hands": "One hand resting on railing; other holding sunglasses"
  },
  "location": {
    "setting": "Balcony overlooking {argument name="location setting" default="Fairmont Hairpin"}",
    "background": "Hairpin curve, red-and-white kerbing, hillside apartments"
  },
  "typography": {
    "text": "UBS, Heineken 0.0 on track barriers"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "Natural daylight",
    "quality": "Soft, evenly lit, low contrast"
```

```
      "hands": "ring visible on left hand, natural finger positioning",

        "skirt": "patterned reddish skirt with detailed textile texture"
      },
      "hair": "long wavy blonde hair cascading over shoulders, individual strands visible",
      "expression": "calm, contemplative, slightly upward gaze",
      "emotion": "intimate, introspective"
    }
  },
  "environment": {
    "setting": "interior space near an open doorway",
```

```
Standing front-facing full body pose, neutral expression, blazer hanging off the arms.

Standing back-facing pose with the head turned toward the camera, blazer worn on the shoulders, legs straight.

Squatting or semi-crouching pose with one leg forward, sharp gaze toward the camera.

Seated low pose with knees bent, body leaning slightly forward, blazer worn on one arm only.
```
